USERMESSAGE #10
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→# hey-chill-qa
     2→
     3→Playwright regression suite for the [Hey Chill](https://hey-chill.vercel.app) PWA.
     4→
     5→## What's tested
     6→
     7→| Suite | Tests | Covers |
     8→|---|---|---|
     9→| `ui.spec.ts` | 8 | Page structure, initial element states, a11y attributes |
    10→| `settings.spec.ts` | 8 | Settings modal open/close/save, localStorage persistence |
    11→| `push-to-talk.spec.ts` | 8 | Mic button toggle, recording state UI |
    12→| `transcription.spec.ts` | 8 | Live transcript updates, HTML escaping, discard flow |
    13→| `vad.spec.ts` | 5 | 3500 ms silence auto-stop (fake timers), timer reset on speech |
    14→| `webhook.spec.ts` | 9 | Webhook POST payload, status labels, error handling |
    15→| `pwa.spec.ts` | 9 | manifest.json, service worker registration, meta tags |
    16→
    17→**Total: 56 tests**
    18→
    19→## Key design decisions
    20→
    21→- **MockSpeechRecognition** — Web Speech API is not available in headless Chromium. A controllable mock is injected via `page.addInitScript()` before every page load. Tests control speech via `window.__mockRecognition._fireResult()`.
    22→- **Fake timers** — VAD tests use `page.clock.install()` + `page.clock.runFor()` so the 3500 ms silence timer fires instantly without real waiting.
    23→- **Network interception** — Webhook tests use `page.route()` to intercept fetch calls; no real webhook is hit.
    24→
    25→## Running the tests
    26→
    27→```bash
    28→# Install dependencies
    29→npm install
    30→
    31→# Install Playwright browser
    32→npx playwright install chromium
    33→
    34→# Run all tests (headless)
    35→npm test
    36→
    37→# Run with headed browser (for debugging)
    38→npm run test:headed
    39→
    40→# Open interactive UI mode
    41→npm run test:ui
    42→
    43→# View last HTML report
    44→npm run test:report
    45→```
    46→
    47→## CI
    48→
    49→Tests run on every push/PR to `main` via `.github/workflows/playwright.yml`.
    50→A scheduled run fires daily at 06:00 UTC to catch upstream regressions on the live deployment.
    51→

USERMESSAGE #16
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→import { test as base, Page } from '@playwright/test';
     2→
     3→export const APP_URL = 'https://hey-chill.vercel.app';
     4→
     5→/**
     6→ * Script injected before page load to replace Web Speech API with a
     7→ * controllable mock. Exposes window.__mockRecognition for test control.
     8→ */
     9→export const MOCK_SPEECH_SCRIPT = `
    10→(function() {
    11→  class MockSpeechRecognition {
    12→    constructor() {
    13→      this.continuous = false;
    14→      this.interimResults = false;
    15→      this.lang = '';
    16→      this.maxAlternatives = 1;
    17→      this.onstart = null;
    18→      this.onresult = null;
    19→      this.onerror = null;
    20→      this.onend = null;
    21→      this._started = false;
    22→      window.__mockRecognition = this;
    23→    }
    24→
    25→    start() {
    26→      this._started = true;
    27→      if (this.onstart) this.onstart();
    28→    }
    29→
    30→    stop() {
    31→      this._started = false;
    32→      if (this.onend) this.onend();
    33→    }
    34→
    35→    /** Simulate a speech result event */
    36→    _fireResult(transcript, isFinal) {
    37→      if (!this.onresult) return;
    38→      const results = [[{ transcript: transcript }]];
    39→      results[0].isFinal = !!isFinal;
    40→      results.length = 1;
    41→      this.onresult({ resultIndex: 0, results: results });
    42→    }
    43→
    44→    /** Simulate a recognition error */
    45→    _fireError(errorCode) {
    46→      if (this.onerror) this.onerror({ error: errorCode });
    47→    }
    48→
    49→    /** Simulate recognition ending on its own (e.g. network cut) */
    50→    _fireEnd() {
    51→      if (this.onend) this.onend();
    52→    }
    53→  }
    54→
    55→  window.SpeechRecognition = MockSpeechRecognition;
    56→  window.webkitSpeechRecognition = MockSpeechRecognition;
    57→})();
    58→`;
    59→
    60→/** Navigate to the app with MockSpeechRecognition pre-installed. */
    61→export async function gotoWithMock(page: Page) {
    62→  await page.addInitScript(MOCK_SPEECH_SCRIPT);
    63→  await page.goto(APP_URL);
    64→}
    65→
    66→/** Simulate a final speech result via the mock. */
    67→export async function simulateSpeech(page: Page, transcript: string) {
    68→  await page.evaluate(
    69→    (t) => (window as any).__mockRecognition._fireResult(t, true),
    70→    transcript,
    71→  );
    72→}
    73→
    74→/** Simulate an interim (non-final) speech result. */
    75→export async function simulateInterim(page: Page, transcript: string) {
    76→  await page.evaluate(
    77→    (t) => (window as any).__mockRecognition._fireResult(t, false),
    78→    transcript,
    79→  );
    80→}
    81→
    82→/** Click mic to start recording, wait for aria-pressed=true. */
    83→export async function startRecording(page: Page) {
    84→  await page.click('#mic-btn');
    85→  await page.waitForFunction(
    86→    () => document.getElementById('mic-btn')?.getAttribute('aria-pressed') === 'true',
    87→  );
    88→}
    89→
    90→/** Click mic to stop recording, wait for aria-pressed=false. */
    91→export async function stopRecording(page: Page) {
    92→  await page.click('#mic-btn');
    93→  await page.waitForFunction(
    94→    () => document.getElementById('mic-btn')?.getAttribute('aria-pressed') === 'false',
    95→  );
    96→}
    97→
    98→// Custom fixture type
    99→type Fixtures = {
   100→  mockPage: Page;
   101→};
   102→
   103→/** A page fixture that pre-installs the mock and navigates to the app. */
   104→export const test = base.extend<Fixtures>({
   105→  mockPage: async ({ page }, use) => {
   106→    await gotoWithMock(page);
   107→    await use(page);
   108→  },
   109→});
   110→
   111→export { expect } from '@playwright/test';
   112→

     1→/**
     2→ * Voice Activity Detection (VAD) Tests
     3→ * Tests the 3500 ms silence auto-stop using page.clock fake timers.
     4→ *
     5→ * Strategy: page.clock.install() before navigation so that setTimeout calls
     6→ * in app.js use fake time. The MockSpeechRecognition is also injected via
     7→ * addInitScript before load.
     8→ */
     9→import { test as base, expect } from '@playwright/test';
    10→import { APP_URL, MOCK_SPEECH_SCRIPT, startRecording } from './fixtures';
    11→
    12→// VAD tests need clock installed before navigation — use a custom setup
    13→const test = base;
    14→
    15→test.describe('VAD silence auto-stop', () => {
    16→  test('auto-stops recording after 3500 ms of silence', async ({ page }) => {
    17→    await page.clock.install();
    18→    await page.addInitScript(MOCK_SPEECH_SCRIPT);
    19→    await page.goto(APP_URL);
    20→
    21→    await startRecording(page);
    22→    await expect(page.locator('#mic-btn')).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');
    23→
    24→    await page.clock.runFor(3500);
    25→
    26→    await expect(page.locator('#mic-btn')).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
    27→  });
    28→
    29→  test('silence timer resets when speech arrives, delaying auto-stop', async ({ page }) => {
    30→    await page.clock.install();
    31→    await page.addInitScript(MOCK_SPEECH_SCRIPT);
    32→    await page.goto(APP_URL);
    33→
    34→    await startRecording(page);
    35→
    36→    // Advance 2000 ms — still within the first 3500 ms window
    37→    await page.clock.runFor(2000);
    38→    await expect(page.locator('#mic-btn')).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');
    39→
    40→    // Speech arrives — resets the 3500 ms timer
    41→    await page.evaluate(() => (window as any).__mockRecognition._fireResult('hello', true));
    42→
    43→    // Advance another 2000 ms (total 4000 ms, but only 2000 since last speech)
    44→    await page.clock.runFor(2000);
    45→    // Should still be recording
    46→    await expect(page.locator('#mic-btn')).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');
    47→
    48→    // Advance the remaining 1500 ms — total 3500 ms after last speech
    49→    await page.clock.runFor(1500);
    50→    await expect(page.locator('#mic-btn')).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
    51→  });
    52→
    53→  test('after VAD auto-stop, transcript bar shows the captured text', async ({ page }) => {
    54→    await page.clock.install();
    55→    await page.addInitScript(MOCK_SPEECH_SCRIPT);
    56→    await page.goto(APP_URL);
    57→
    58→    await startRecording(page);
    59→    await page.evaluate(() => (window as any).__mockRecognition._fireResult('voice activity test', true));
    60→
    61→    await page.clock.runFor(3500);
    62→
    63→    await expect(page.locator('#transcript-bar')).toBeVisible();
    64→    await expect(page.locator('#transcript-text')).toContainText('voice activity test');
    65→  });
    66→
    67→  test('manual stop clears the silence timer (no double-stop)', async ({ page }) => {
    68→    await page.clock.install();
    69→    await page.addInitScript(MOCK_SPEECH_SCRIPT);
    70→    await page.goto(APP_URL);
    71→
    72→    await startRecording(page);
    73→    await page.evaluate(() => (window as any).__mockRecognition._fireResult('manual stop', true));
    74→

    76→    await page.click('#mic-btn');
    77→    await expect(page.locator('#mic-btn')).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
    78→
    79→    // Advance past 3500 ms — should not cause errors or state flipping

    81→    await expect(page.locator('#mic-btn')).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
    82→    await expect(page.locator('#transcript-bar')).toBeVisible();
    83→  });

    51→function getAudioContext() {
    52→  if (!audioCtx) {
    53→    audioCtx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    54→  }
    55→  if (audioCtx.state === 'suspended') {
    56→    audioCtx.resume();
    57→  }
    58→  return audioCtx;
    59→}
    60→
    61→// Prime the AudioContext on first user interaction so it's ready for hands-free sends
    62→function primeAudio() {
    63→  try { getAudioContext(); } catch (_) {}
    64→}
    65→
    66→function _playTone(ctx, frequency, startTime, duration, gain) {
    67→  const osc  = ctx.createOscillator();
    68→  const amp  = ctx.createGain();
    69→  osc.connect(amp);
    70→  amp.connect(ctx.destination);
    71→  osc.type = 'sine';
    72→  osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(frequency, startTime);
    73→  amp.gain.setValueAtTime(0, startTime);
    74→  amp.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(gain, startTime + 0.01);
    75→  amp.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, startTime + duration);
    76→  osc.start(startTime);
    77→  osc.stop(startTime + duration);
    78→}
    79→
    80→function playSuccessSound() {
    81→  // Prefer speech synthesis — "Got it" is immediately understood
    82→  if ('speechSynthesis' in window) {
    83→    const utt = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance('Got it');
    84→    utt.rate   = 1.1;
    85→    utt.pitch  = 1.1;
    86→    utt.volume = 1;
    87→    window.speechSynthesis.speak(utt);
    88→    return;
    89→  }
    90→  // Fallback: ascending double chime
    91→  try {
    92→    const ctx = getAudioContext();
    93→    const now = ctx.currentTime;
    94→    _playTone(ctx, 880,  now,        0.22, 0.30); // A5
    95→    _playTone(ctx, 1320, now + 0.18, 0.38, 0.25); // E6
    96→  } catch (e) {
    97→    console.warn('Audio playback failed:', e);
    98→  }
    99→}
   100→
   101→function playFailureSound() {
   102→  // Descending dissonant triple-tone — distinct "uh-oh" signal
   103→  try {
   104→    const ctx = getAudioContext();

   107→    _playTone(ctx, 262, now + 0.15, 0.18, 0.40); // C4
   108→    _playTone(ctx, 196, now + 0.30, 0.45, 0.35); // G3
   109→  } catch (e) {
   110→    console.warn('Audio playback failed:', e);
   111→  }
   112→}

   119→/* ===== Speech Recognition setup ===== */
   120→const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
   121→
   122→if (!SpeechRecognition) {
   123→  notSupported.hidden = false;
   124→  quickBtn.disabled = true;
   125→  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');

   127→  brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
   128→} else {

   130→}
   131→
   132→function initRecognition() {
   133→  recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
   134→  recognition.continuous     = true;
   135→  recognition.interimResults = true;
   136→  recognition.lang           = navigator.language || 'en-US';
   137→  recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;
   138→
   139→  recognition.onstart = () => {
   140→    if (_brainstormRestarting) {
   141→      // Seamless brainstorm restart — preserve accumulated transcript, don't reset UI
   142→      isListening = true;
   143→      finalTranscript = brainstormAccumulator;
   144→      interimText = '';
   145→      _brainstormRestarting = false;
   146→      return;
   147→    }
   148→    isListening = true;
   149→    finalTranscript = '';
   150→    brainstormAccumulator = '';
   151→    interimText = '';
   152→    setRecordingUI(true, activeMode);
   153→  };
   154→
   155→  recognition.onresult = (event) => {
   156→    let interim = '';
   157→    for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
   158→      const result = event.results[i];
   159→      if (result.isFinal) {
   160→        finalTranscript += result[0].transcript + ' ';
   161→      } else {
   162→        interim += result[0].transcript;
   163→      }
   164→    }
   165→    interimText = interim;
   166→    const displayText = (finalTranscript + interim).trim();
   167→    updateLiveText(displayText);
   168→
   169→    // Silence timer only applies to quick mode
   170→    if (activeMode === 'quick') {
   171→      resetSilenceTimer();
   172→    }
   173→  };
   174→
   175→  recognition.onerror = (event) => {
   176→    // 'no-speech' is common and expected — just stop cleanly
   177→    if (event.error !== 'no-speech') {
   178→      console.warn('Speech recognition error:', event.error);
   179→    }
   180→    _brainstormRestarting = false;
   181→    stopListening();
   182→  };
   183→
   184→  recognition.onend = () => {
   185→    if (isListening && activeMode === 'brainstorm') {
   186→      // Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically — restart seamlessly
   187→      brainstormAccumulator = finalTranscript;
   188→      _brainstormRestarting = true;
   189→      setTimeout(() => {
   190→        if (isListening && activeMode === 'brainstorm') {
   191→          try {
   192→            recognition.start();
   193→          } catch (_) {
   194→            _brainstormRestarting = false;
   195→            brainstormAccumulator = '';
   196→            isListening = false;
   197→            finishRecording();
   198→          }
   199→        } else {
   200→          _brainstormRestarting = false;
   201→        }
   202→      }, 150);
   203→      return;
   204→    }
   205→    // onend fires when recognition stops for any reason
   206→    if (isListening) {
   207→      // We didn't call stop manually yet; auto-stop happened
   208→      finishRecording();
   209→    }
   210→  };
   211→}
   212→
   213→function resetSilenceTimer() {
   214→  clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
   215→  silenceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   216→    if (isListening) stopListening();
   217→  }, SILENCE_DELAY);
   218→}
   219→
   220→/* ===== Recording controls ===== */
   221→function startListening(mode) {
   222→  if (!recognition || isListening) return;
   223→  activeMode = mode;
   224→  hideTranscriptBar();
   225→
   226→  // Ensure wake recognition is stopped before starting main recording
   227→  if (wakeMode) stopWakeRecognition();
   228→
   229→  try {
   230→    recognition.start();
   231→  } catch (e) {
   232→    console.warn('Could not start recognition:', e);
   233→    // Re-init in case of invalid state
   234→    initRecognition();
   235→    try { recognition.start(); } catch (_) {}
   236→  }
   237→
   238→  if (mode === 'quick') {
   239→    resetSilenceTimer();
   240→  }
   241→}
   242→
   243→function stopListening() {
   244→  clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
   245→  _brainstormRestarting = false; // prevent auto-restart in brainstorm
   246→  isListening = false; // mark before calling stop so onend doesn't re-trigger finishRecording
   247→  if (recognition) {
   248→    try { recognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}
   249→  }
   250→  finishRecording();
   251→}
   252→
   253→function finishRecording() {
   254→  const mode = activeMode;
   255→  setRecordingUI(false, mode);
   256→  const text = finalTranscript.trim();
   257→  brainstormAccumulator = '';
   258→  activeMode = null;
   259→  if (text) {
   260→    if (wakeTriggeredRecording) {
   261→      // Hands-free path: auto-send without requiring a tap
   262→      sendMessage(text);
   263→    } else {
   264→      showTranscriptBar(text);
   265→    }
   266→  }
   267→  wakeTriggeredRecording = false;
   268→  // Resume passive wake word listening if mode is active
   269→  if (wakeMode) scheduleWakeRestart();
   270→  updateWakeHint();
   271→}
   272→
   273→/* ===== UI state helpers ===== */
   274→function setRecordingUI(recording, mode) {

   289→

   309→

   364→/* ===== Webhook send ===== */
   365→async function sendMessage(text) {
   366→  const webhookUrl = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';
   367→  const timestamp  = new Date().toISOString();
   368→  const payload    = { text, source: 'hey-chill', timestamp };
   369→
   370→  // Add message to history immediately
   371→  const msgEl = addMessage(text, timestamp, 'sending');
   372→
   373→  if (!webhookUrl) {
   374→    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'no-webhook');
   375→    return;
   376→  }
   377→
   378→  try {
   379→    const res = await fetch(webhookUrl, {
   380→      method: 'POST',
   381→      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   382→      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
   383→    });
   384→    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
   385→    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'sent');
   386→    playSuccessSound();
   387→  } catch (err) {
   388→    console.warn('Webhook error:', err);
   389→    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'error');
   390→    playFailureSound();
   391→  }
   392→}
   393→
   394→/* ===== Message history ===== */
   395→function addMessage(text, timestamp, status) {
   396→  // Hide empty state
   397→  messagesEmpty.style.display = 'none';
   398→
   399→  const el = document.createElement('div');
   400→  el.className = `message ${status}`;
   401→
   402→  const timeStr = new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], {
   403→    hour: '2-digit',
   404→    minute: '2-digit',
   405→  });
   406→
   407→  const statusLabel = {
   408→    sending:    'Sending…',
   409→    sent:       'Sent',
   410→    error:      'Failed',
   411→    'no-webhook': 'No webhook',
   412→  };
   413→
   414→  el.innerHTML = `
   415→    <p class="message-text">${escapeHtml(text)}</p>
   416→    <div class="message-meta">
   417→      <span class="message-time">${timeStr}</span>
   418→      <span class="message-status">${statusLabel[status] || status}</span>
   419→    </div>
   420→  `;
   421→
   422→  messagesEl.appendChild(el);
   423→  el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'end' });
   424→  return el;
   425→}
   426→
   427→function updateMessageStatus(el, status) {
   428→  el.className = `message ${status}`;
   429→  const statusEl = el.querySelector('.message-status');
   430→  const labels = {
   431→    sent:         'Sent',
   432→    error:        'Failed',
   433→    'no-webhook': 'No webhook set',
   434→  };
   435→  if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = labels[status] || status;
   436→}
   437→
   438→function escapeHtml(str) {
   439→  return str
   440→    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
   441→    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
   442→    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
   443→    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
   444→    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
   445→}
   446→
   447→/* ===== Settings modal ===== */
   448→settingsBtn.addEventListener('click', openSettings);
   449→modalClose.addEventListener('click',  closeSettings);
   450→modalOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   451→  if (e.target === modalOverlay) closeSettings();
   452→});
   453→
   454→document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {

   463→
   464→function openSettings() {
   465→  webhookInput.value = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';
   466→  modalOverlay.hidden = false;
   467→  webhookInput.focus();
   468→}
   469→
   470→function closeSettings() {
   471→  modalOverlay.hidden = true;
   472→}
   473→
   474→/* ===== Wake Word Detection ===== */
   475→
   476→function isWakePhrase(transcript) {
   477→  return WAKE_PHRASES.some(phrase => transcript.includes(phrase));
   478→}
   479→
   480→function initWakeRecognition() {
   481→  wakeRecognition = new SpeechRecognition();
   482→  wakeRecognition.continuous     = true;
   483→  wakeRecognition.interimResults = true;
   484→  wakeRecognition.lang           = navigator.language || 'en-US';
   485→  wakeRecognition.maxAlternatives = 1;
   486→
   487→  wakeRecognition.onresult = (event) => {
   488→    for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
   489→      const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript.toLowerCase().trim();
   490→      if (isWakePhrase(transcript)) {
   491→        handleWakeWordDetected();
   492→        return;
   493→      }
   494→    }
   495→  };
   496→
   497→  wakeRecognition.onerror = (event) => {
   498→    if (event.error === 'not-allowed' || event.error === 'service-not-allowed') {
   499→      // Microphone access denied — silently disable wake mode
   500→      disableWakeMode();
   501→      return;
   502→    }
   503→    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
   504→      scheduleWakeRestart();
   505→    }
   506→  };
   507→
   508→  wakeRecognition.onend = () => {
   509→    // Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically — restart unless we
   510→    // deliberately stopped it to hand off to main recording.
   511→    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
   512→      scheduleWakeRestart();
   513→    }
   514→  };
   515→}
   516→
   517→function startWakeRecognition() {
   518→  if (!wakeRecognition) initWakeRecognition();
   519→  wakeTriggered = false;
   520→  quickRing.classList.add('listening-passive'); // passive glow on quick button only
   521→  try {
   522→    wakeRecognition.start();
   523→  } catch (e) {
   524→    // InvalidStateError when already started — reinit and retry
   525→    initWakeRecognition();
   526→    try { wakeRecognition.start(); } catch (_) {}
   527→  }
   528→}
   529→
   530→function stopWakeRecognition() {
   531→  quickRing.classList.remove('listening-passive');
   532→  if (wakeRecognition) {
   533→    try { wakeRecognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}
   534→  }
   535→}
   536→
   537→function scheduleWakeRestart() {
   538→  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);
   539→  wakeRestartTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   540→    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
   541→      startWakeRecognition();
   542→    }
   543→  }, 300);
   544→}
   545→
   546→function handleWakeWordDetected() {
   547→  if (isListening || wakeTriggered) return;
   548→  wakeTriggered = true;
   549→  wakeTriggeredRecording = true; // flag so finishRecording auto-sends
   550→  stopWakeRecognition();
   551→  // Give the recognition engine a moment to fully stop before starting main recording
   552→  setTimeout(() => {
   553→    wakeTriggered = false;
   554→    startListening('quick'); // wake word always triggers quick mode
   555→  }, 250);
   556→}
   557→
   558→function enableWakeMode() {
   559→  wakeMode = true;
   560→  wakeBtn.classList.add('wake-active');
   561→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');
   562→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Disable wake word');
   563→  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: ON';
   564→  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '1');
   565→  updateWakeHint();
   566→  if (!isListening) startWakeRecognition();
   567→}
   568→
   569→function disableWakeMode() {
   570→  wakeMode = false;
   571→  wakeBtn.classList.remove('wake-active');
   572→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
   573→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Enable wake word');
   574→  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: Hey Chill';
   575→  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '0');
   576→  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);
   577→  stopWakeRecognition();
   578→  updateWakeHint();
   579→}
   580→
   581→function updateWakeHint() {
   582→  if (!isListening) {
   583→    micHint.textContent = wakeMode ? 'Say "Hey Chill" or tap Quick' : '';
   584→    micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active');
   585→  }
   586→}
   587→
   588→wakeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   589→  primeAudio();
   590→  if (wakeMode) {
   591→    disableWakeMode();
   592→  } else {
   593→    enableWakeMode();
   594→  }
   595→});
   596→
   597→// Restore wake mode preference across sessions
   598→if (SpeechRecognition && localStorage.getItem('wakeMode') === '1') {
   599→  enableWakeMode();
   600→}
   601→

Page loads \u2192 two buttons visible side-by-side (\"Quick\", \"Brainstorm\")\n *  2. Quick button \u2192 starts recording (aria-pressed=true), auto-stops after 3500 ms silence\n *  3. Brainstorm button \u2192 starts recording, does NOT auto-stop on silence\n *  4. Brainstorm \u2192 tap again to manually stop \u2192 shows transcript\n *  5. Only one mode can be active at a time\n *  6. ARIA labels are correct on load and during recording\n *  7. Hint text changes correctly per active mode\n *  8. Buttons fit side-by-side on a 360 px mobile viewport (no overflow)\n *  9. Wake word \"Hey Chill\" triggers Quick mode specifically\n */\n\nimport { test as base, expect, Page } from '@playwright/test';\nimport { MOCK_SPEECH_SCRIPT } from './fixtures';\n\n/* ===== Constants ===== */\nconst PR_URL = 'http://localhost:9090';\n\n/**\n * Enhanced mock that tracks every SpeechRecognition instance created so tests\n * can target the wake-word recognition separately from the main recognition.\n * window.__mockInstances[0] \u2192 main recognition\n * window.__mockInstances[1] \u2192 wake recognition (created after wake mode enabled)\n */\nconst MULTI_INSTANCE_MOCK_SCRIPT = `\n(function() {\n  const instances = [];\n\n  class MockSpeechRecognition {\n    constructor() {\n      this.continuous = false;\n      this.interimResults = false;\n      this.lang = '';\n      this.maxAlternatives = 1;\n      this.onstart = null;\n      this.onresult = null;\n      this.onerror = null;\n      this.onend = null;\n      this._started = false;\n      instances.push(this);\n      window.__mockInstances = instances;\n      window.__mockRecognition = this; // latest instance (convenience)\n    }\n\n    start() {\n      this._started = true;\n      if (this.onstart) this.onstart();\n    }\n\n    stop() {\n      this._started = false;\n      if (this.onend) this.onend();\n    }\n\n    _fireResult(transcript, isFinal) {\n      if (!this.onresult) return;\n      const results = [[{ transcript: transcript }]];\n      results[0].isFinal = !!isFinal;\n      results.length = 1;\n      this.onresult({ resultIndex: 0, results: results });\n    }\n\n    _fireError(errorCode) {\n      if (this.onerror) this.onerror({ error: errorCode });\n    }\n\n    _fireEnd() {\n      if (this.onend) this.onend();\n    }\n  }\n\n  window.SpeechRecognition = MockSpeechRecognition;\n  window.webkitSpeechRecognition = MockSpeechRecognition;\n})();\n`;\n\n/* ===== Helpers ===== */\n\nasync function gotoWithMock(page: Page) {\n  await );\n}\n\nasync function startQuick(page: Page) {\n  await page.click('#quick-btn');\n  await page.waitForFunction(\n    () => document.getElementById('quick-btn')?.getAttribute('aria-pressed') === Wake word triggers Quick mode specifically\n * ================================================================ */\n\ntest.describe('Wake word integration', () => {\n  test('\"Hey Chill\" wake phrase starts Quick mode, not Brainstorm', async ({ page }) => {\n    await page.clock.install();\n    await page.addInitScript(MULTI_INSTANCE_MOCK_SCRIPT);\n    await page.goto(PR_URL);\n\n    // Enable wake mode \u2014 this creates a second SpeechRecognition instance (wakeRecognition)\n    await page.click('#wake-btn');\n\n    // Wait for wake recognition instance to be created and started\n    await page.waitForFunction(() => (window as any).__mockInstances?.length >= 2);\n\n    // Fire the wake phrase on the wake recognition instance (index 1)\n    await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const wakeRecognition = (window as any).__mockInstances[1];\n      wakeRecognition._fireResult('hey chill', false); // interim transcript is sufficient\n    });\n\n    // handleWakeWordDetected uses setTimeout(250 ms) before calling startListening('quick')\n    await page.clock.runFor(300);\n\n    // Quick must now be recording\n    await expect(page.locator('#quick-btn')).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');\n\n    // Brainstorm must NOT be recording\n    await expect(page.locator('#brainstorm-btn')).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');\n  });\n\n  test('wake hint text shows when wake mode is enabled', async ({ mockPage: page }) => {\n    await page.click('#wake-btn');\n    await expect(page.locator('#mic-hint')).toHaveText('Say \"Hey Chill\" or tap Quick');\n  });\n});\n"
    },
    "caller": {
      "type": "direct"
    }
  }

USERMESSAGE #88
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→# hey-chill-qa
     2→
     3→Playwright regression suite for the [Hey Chill](https://hey-chill.vercel.app) PWA.
     4→
     5→## What's tested
     6→
     7→| Suite | Tests | Covers |
     8→|---|---|---|
     9→| `ui.spec.ts` | 8 | Page structure, initial element states, a11y attributes |
    10→| `settings.spec.ts` | 8 | Settings modal open/close/save, localStorage persistence |
    11→| `push-to-talk.spec.ts` | 8 | Mic button toggle, recording state UI |
    12→| `transcription.spec.ts` | 8 | Live transcript updates, HTML escaping, discard flow |
    13→| `vad.spec.ts` | 5 | 3500 ms silence auto-stop (fake timers), timer reset on speech |
    14→| `webhook.spec.ts` | 9 | Webhook POST payload, status labels, error handling |
    15→| `pwa.spec.ts` | 9 | manifest.json, service worker registration, meta tags |
    16→
    17→**Total: 56 tests**
    18→
    19→## Key design decisions
    20→
    21→- **MockSpeechRecognition** — Web Speech API is not available in headless Chromium. A controllable mock is injected via `page.addInitScript()` before every page load. Tests control speech via `window.__mockRecognition._fireResult()`.
    22→- **Fake timers** — VAD tests use `page.clock.install()` + `page.clock.runFor()` so the 3500 ms silence timer fires instantly without real waiting.
    23→- **Network interception** — Webhook tests use `page.route()` to intercept fetch calls; no real webhook is hit.
    24→
    25→## Running the tests
    26→
    27→```bash
    28→# Install dependencies
    29→npm install
    30→
    31→# Install Playwright browser
    32→npx playwright install chromium
    33→
    34→# Run all tests (headless)
    35→npm test
    36→
    37→# Run with headed browser (for debugging)
    38→npm run test:headed
    39→
    40→# Open interactive UI mode
    41→npm run test:ui
    42→
    43→# View last HTML report
    44→npm run test:report
    45→```
    46→
    47→## CI
    48→
    49→Tests run on every push/PR to `main` via `.github/workflows/playwright.yml`.
    50→A scheduled run fires daily at 06:00 UTC to catch upstream regressions on the live deployment.
    51→

 ## Key design decisions
 
 - **MockSpeechRecognition** — Web Speech API is not available in headless Chromium. A controllable mock is injected via `page.addInitScript()` before every page load. Tests control speech via `window.__mockRecognition._fireResult()`.
+- **Multi-instance mock** — `dual-mode-ui.spec.ts` uses an enhanced mock (`MULTI_INSTANCE_MOCK_SCRIPT`) that tracks all `SpeechRecognition` instances in `window.__mockInstances`. `[0]` is the main recognition; `[1]` is the wake-word recognition created when wake mode is enabled.
 - **Fake timers** — VAD tests use `page.clock.install()` + `page.clock.runFor()` so the 3500 ms silence timer fires instantly without real waiting.
 - **Network interception** — Webhook tests use `page.route()` to intercept fetch calls; no real webhook is hit.
+- **Dual-mode target** — `dual-mode-ui.spec.ts` runs against `http://localhost:9090` (the `feature/FRG-211-dual-mode-ui-quick-brainstorm` branch served locally) rather than the production URL.

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #104
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `tests/dual-mode-ui.spec.ts` — New file: 27 Playwright tests covering all FRG-211 acceptance criteria (layout, Quick mode, Brainstorm mode, hint text, mutual exclusion, wake word). Tests run against `http://localhost:9090` (PR branch cloned and served locally). - `README.md` — Updated test table (56 → 83 total), added multi-instance mock and dual-mode target to design decisions. ## Key Decisions - **Multi-instance mock** (`MULTI_INSTANCE_MOCK_SCRIPT`): the PR app creates two separate `SpeechRecognition` instances — one for main recording, one for wake-word detection. A tracking array (`window.__mockInstances`) lets tests fire "hey chill" on the wake recognition (`[1]`) without clobbering the main recording mock (`[0]`). - **Fake clocks for VAD/brainstorm no-VAD tests**: `page.clock.install()` + `page.clock.runFor(3500)` used so brainstorm's "no VAD" assertion is instant and deterministic, not a 3.5 s real wait. - **360px viewport test** uses `page.setViewportSize()` + bounding box checks rather than a CSS snapshot, giving a concrete pixel-level assertion about overflow. - All 27 new tests passed on first run; all 56 existing regression tests continue to pass. ## PR / Branch - Pushed directly to `main` on the QA repo (`chillkimtest-oss/hey-chill-qa`), commit `7475520`.

A tracking array (`window.__mockInstances`) lets tests fire \"hey chill\" on the wake recognition (`[1]`) without clobbering the main recording mock (`[0]`).\n- **Fake clocks for VAD/brainstorm no-VAD tests**: `page.clock.install()` + `page.clock.runFor(3500)` used so brainstorm's \"no VAD\" assertion is instant and deterministic, not a 3.5 s real wait.\n- **360px viewport test** uses `page.setViewportSize()` + bounding box checks rather than a CSS snapshot, giving a concrete pixel-level assertion about overflow.\n- All 27 new tests passed on first run; all 56 existing regression tests continue to pass.\n\n## PR / Branch\n- Pushed directly to `main` on the QA repo (`chillkimtest-oss/hey-chill-qa`), commit `7475520`."
